    <div id="js-article-text" class="article-text wide">
        <h1>Friends of girl, 18, with leukemia sign her casket with loving messages in a final goodbye after she died waiting for a hospital bed during a shortage in Canada</h1>
<ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Laura Hillier, 18, died after waiting for a bone marrow transplant during a hospital bed shortage in <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/canada/index.html">Canada</a>, despite having willing donors availableÂ </strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>An Ontario hospital said it could only do five transplants a month and there were about 30 people who were waiting to have the procedure done</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>At her funeral, friends and family signed her casket with loving messagesÂ </strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>The Hillier family is now fighting in Laura's memory to end 'deadly' wait times for hospital beds in Canada</strong></font></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Kalhan+Rosenblatt+For+Dailymail.com" class="author" rel="nofollow">Kalhan Rosenblatt For Dailymail.com</a>


</p>

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><div class="mol-img-group floatRHS">    <div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-cfe64cbd83c51ac6" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/06/17/30F21ABA00000578-3435131-image-a-45_1454781323689.jpg" height="383" width="306" alt="Laura Hillier (pictured), who had leukemia, died after waiting for a bed to become available in a Canadian hospital for a bone marrow transplantÂ " class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">Laura Hillier (pictured), who had leukemia, died after waiting for a bed to become available in a Canadian hospital for a bone marrow transplantÂ </p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">A girl who died of leukemia was given a final send off after her friends signed her casket with loving messages on January 30.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Laura Hillier got to experience a few normal childhood milestones like graduating high school and getting her senior year book signed before she died on January 20.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"><span class="mol-style-bold">Scroll down for videoÂ </span></font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Laura might have experienced a few more milestones if a Hamilton, Ontario, <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/canada/index.html">Canada</a>, hospital had been able to accommodate a bone marrow transplant for the young woman.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Numerous donors were a match with Laura and ready to donate, but Hamilton's Juravinski Hospital didn't have enough beds in high-air-pressure rooms for the procedure.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Hospital staff told her they had about 30 patients with potential donors, but the means to only do about five transplants a month.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Laura was first diagnosed with acute myeloid leukemia at age 13.Â </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">She had been completely cancer-free for approximately four years after her first battle with AML, and relapsed this past May.Â </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Though Laura was able to achieve remission for a second time, she relapsed again in November 2015.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"></font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Dr. Ralph Meyer, Juravinski's vice-president of oncology and palliative care, told Ontario's <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" rel="nofollow" href="http://www.thestar.com/life/health_wellness/2015/07/12/wait-for-hospital-bed-keeps-leukemia-patients-transplant-on-hold-despite-multiple-matches.html">TheStar.com</a> there are plenty of others facing the same situation as Laura in Canada.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">He said donor registries are growing in size, and technological advances allow transplants to safely happen between people who are less of a match for each other are becoming more and more common.</font></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <img </div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'It is crazy to have to be on a wait-list when you have a donor and you are ready to go,' Laura told TheStar.com in July of 2015.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Putting off the surgery meant Laura had to endure her fifth round of painstaking chemotherapy.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">After her death in January, her obituary slammed Canada's bed shortage as having 'deadly wait times':</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'In Laura's last year with us, she was determined to bring public attention to the problem of deadly wait times for bone marrow transplants in Ontario and across Canada.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'In July 2015, Laura achieved remission for the second time from acute myeloid leukemia and was blessed to have a perfect donor match.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'However, she found out that she would not be able to receive her life-saving transplant for months as there were many waiting ahead of her and not enough resources to handle the demand.'</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">After her death, the outpouring of love was so great for Laura, her family asked some people to only attend the visitation, rather than the funeral, because they were worried about running out of room.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Friends of the musical theater-loving teen came out in droves, signing the casket in marker, talking about her life and singing songs.Â </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'Though Laura's casket was a beautiful sentiment from her friends and family, Laura's fight, and now our fight, is to change the medical system to end the deadly wait times for patients requiring a bone marrow transplant,' a post on the Hope for Laura Hillier Facebook page said.</font></p><div class="artSplitter <script async src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 10.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
